[30;1m199 | [0m[35mTiming in MIDI files is centered around ticks. Each message in a MIDI file has[0m
[30;1m200 | [0m[35ma delta time, which tells how many ticks have passed since the last message.[0m
[30;1m201 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m202 | [0m[35mA tick is the smallest unit of time in MIDI and remains fixed throughout the[0m
[30;1m203 | [0m[35msong. Each quarter notes is divided into a certain number of ticks, often[0m
[30;1m204 | [0m[35mreferred as the resolution of the file or pulses per quarter note (PPQN). This[0m
[30;1m205 | [0m[35mresolution is stored as ``ticks_per_beat`` in MidiFile objects.[0m
